***кресло.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кресло.html>кре́сло</a> (803)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*krěslo</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кресло.html>кре́сло</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kréslo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кресло.html>кре́сла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кресло.html>кре́сла</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кресло.html>кре́сел</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>armchair, easy chair</li>
<li>theater stall</li>
<li>responsible position, post</li></ol>

***крест.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:крест.html>крест</a> (1903)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">крьстъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krĭstŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*krьstъ</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">крёст</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krjost</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the inherited East Slavic form.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крест.html>крест</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">krest</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крест.html>креста́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крест.html>кресты́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крест.html>кресто́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cross
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">крест-на́крест</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">krest-nákrest</i> ― <span class="e-translation">crosswise</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вот.html>вот</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>те</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:крест.html>крест</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vot te krest</i> ― <span class="e-translation">cross my heart</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">criminal  slang<span class="ib-comma">,</span> animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> thief</li></ol>

***крестившийся.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:креститься.html>крести́вшийся</a> (11878)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:креститься.html>крести́вшийся</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">krestívšijsja</span>)
</p>

***крестить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:крестить.html>крести́ть</a> (13983)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*krьstiti</i>. Compare <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">кстить</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kstitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with different treatment of the reduced vowel.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крестить.html>крести́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">krestítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окрестить.html>окрести́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to baptize, to christen</li>
<li>to be a godfather, to be a sponsor</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крестить.html>крести́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">krestítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекрестить.html>перекрести́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cross, to make the sign of the cross on (someone)</li></ol>

<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="религиозное">религ.</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a> восприемником (крёстным <a href = vnd.unilang:отец.html>отцо́м</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> восприемницей (крёстной <a href = vnd.unilang:мать.html>ма́терью</a>) <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>

</ul></li>


<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="религиозное">религ.</span>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> доп.</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершать.html>соверша́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:крестный.html>кре́стное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знамение.html>зна́мение</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:над.html>над</a> чем-либо <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:крестник.html>кре́стник</a> (31410)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крестить.html>крести́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krestítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ник</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:крестовый.html>кресто́вый</a> (19269)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крест.html>крест</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krest</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cross</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́вый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-óvyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крестовый.html>кресто́вый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">krestóvyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cross
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:крестовый.html>кресто́вая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:булочка.html>бу́лочка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>krestóvaja</b> búločka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">hot <b>cross</b> bun</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>cross</b> bun</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> crusade <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">military expedition undertaken by the Christians of Europe in the 11th to 13th centuries</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:крестовый.html>кресто́вый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:поход.html>похо́д</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>krestóvyj</b> poxód</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>crusade</b></span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>crusade</b> campaign</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крестить.html>кре́сти</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krésti</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">clubs</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́вый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-óvyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крестовый.html>кресто́вый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">krestóvyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> clubs <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">card game</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:крестовый.html>кресто́вый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:валет.html>вале́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>krestóvyj</b> valét</i> ― <span class="e-translation">jack of <b>clubs</b></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крест.html>крест</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krest</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cross</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:носить.html>носи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nosítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to carry</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ец</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ec</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крестоносец.html>крестоно́сец</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">krestonósec</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крестоносец.html>крестоно́сца</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крестоносец.html>крестоно́сцы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крестоносец.html>крестоно́сцев</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:крестьянин.html>крестья́нин</a> (1941)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">крьстьꙗнинъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krĭstĭjaninŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Christian; human, person; tax-paying villager</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">крьстьꙗнъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krĭstĭjanŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Christian; peasant, tiller; tax-paying villager</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">christiānus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Christian</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. For semantic shift to "peasant", compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cretin</i>, also from Latin <span class="Latn" lang="la">christiānus</span>, through French.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кривить.html>криви́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:каблук.html>каблуки́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>krivítʹ</b> kablukí</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to twist the heels</span></div></dd>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кривить.html>криви́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krivítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кривиться.html>криви́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">krivítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:искривиться.html>искриви́ться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скривиться.html>скриви́ться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покривиться.html>покриви́ться</a></b>)

<ol><li>to become crooked/bent/lop-sided</li>

***кривлявшийся.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кривляться.html>кривля́вшийся</a> (20673)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***кривой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кривой.html>криво́й</a> (30306)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*krivъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кривой.html>криво́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">krivój</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)криве́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)криве́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>crooked, curved, wry, bent</li>
<li>wrong, false, unfair</li>
<li>one-eyed</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изогнутый.html>изо́гнутый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">izógnutyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неровный.html>неро́вный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">neróvnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***кризис.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кризис.html>кри́зис</a> (3304)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">crisis</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κρίσις</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krísis</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a separating, power of distinguishing, decision, choice, election, judgment, dispute</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κρίνω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krínō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pick out, choose, decide, judge</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***крик.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:крик.html>крик</a> (1044)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*krȋkъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крик.html>крик</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">krik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крик.html>кри́ка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крик.html>кри́ки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крик.html>кри́ков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cry (a shout or scream), outcry, scream, shout, shouting, yell</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крик.html>крик</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ли́вый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lívyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крикливый.html>крикли́вый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kriklívyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>loud</li>
<li>clamorous
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потом.html>Потом</a> Катавасов <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:громкий.html>гро́мким</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:крикливый.html>крикли́вым</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:голос.html>го́лосом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прочесть.html>прочёл</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свою́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:записка.html>запи́ску</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:об.html>об</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ученый.html>учёных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:труд.html>труда́х</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:юбиляр.html>юбиля́ра</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Potom Katavasov svoim gromkim, <b>kriklivym</b> golosom pročel svoju zapisku ob učenyx trudax jubiljara</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Then Katavasov, in his loud, <b>clamorous</b> voice, read his note on the scientific works of the hero of the day.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>garish, flashy
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:крикливый.html>крикли́вая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:реклама.html>рекла́ма</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kriklívaja</b> rekláma</i> ― <span class="e-translation">loud publicity</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***крикнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:крикнуть.html>кри́кнуть</a> (669)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крикнуть.html>кри́кнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kríknutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кричать.html>крича́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cry out, to shout (at) (semelfactive)</li>
<li>to scream</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:позвать.html>позва́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pozvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кликнуть.html>кли́кнуть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">klíknutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><i>See <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кричать.html>крича́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kričátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> for derived verbs.</i></li></ul>

***крикун.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:крикун.html>крику́н</a> (23939)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кричать.html>крича́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kričátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ун</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-un</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крикун.html>крику́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">krikún</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крикун.html>крикуна́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крикун.html>крикуны́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крикун.html>крикуно́в</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">крику́нья</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">крику́шка</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">крику́ха</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> bawler; shouter; screamer, crier  <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">someone who shouts or likes to shout, screams, yells or cries</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>loudmouth; clamo(u)rer; squaller <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">one who talks too much or too loudly, especially in a boastful or self-important manner, someone who makes noise</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> propagandist; someone spreading negative and sometimes false information</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:криминал.html>кримина́л</a> (17974)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:криминал.html>кримина́л</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kriminál</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:криминал.html>кримина́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:криминал.html>кримина́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:криминал.html>кримина́лов</a></b>)
</p>
